<h3 class="cut-tit"><strong><a title="中国好工长" href="http://jiaju.sina.com.cn/gongzhang/bj.shtml">中国好工长</a></strong></h3>
<div class="cut-art">

    var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; s.parentNode.insertBefore(ga, s);
  })();

</script>
</body>
</html>
